class Slot {

   LocalDateTime start
   LocalDateTime end

    Slot(LocalDateTime start, LocalDateTime end) {
        this.start = start
        this.end = end
    }

    @Override
    String toString() {
        return "Slot{" +
                "start=" + start +
                ", end=" + end +
                '}';
    }
}
